# Page 5

ARGENT BIRCH EMPLOYERS | WORKERS COMPENSATION AND EMPLOYERS LIABILITY
Employers Liability General Provisions

YW700400
04/01/2026 - 04/01/2027

EMPLOYERS LIABILITY GENERAL PROVISIONS

WC 04 03 06 policy form                                                     Policy No. YW700400

ITEM,STATE / CLASS
WC-0004,MA / 5190
CLASSIFICATION,PAYROLL / RATE
Electrical wiring within buildings,$77,560 / 2.86
PREMIUM,FORM
$2,218,WC 04 03 06 01 15

EMPLOYERS LIABILITY PROVISIONS ADDRESS THE FINANCIAL CONSEQUENCES OF WORKPLACE INJURIES NOT STRICTLY RESOLVED THROUGH STATUTORY WORKERS COMPENSATION FRAMEWORKS. THIS SECTION APPLIES TO BODILY INJURY BY ACCIDENT OR BODILY INJURY BY DISEASE ARISING OUT OF AND IN THE COURSE OF THE INJURED EMPLOYEE'S EMPLOYMENT BY BLUE KETTLE FOOD SERVICE, LLC. THE INJURY MUST OCCUR DURING THE POLICY PERIOD AND WITHIN THE DESIGNATED COVERAGE TERRITORIES.

The insured entity must immediately forward any demands, notices, summonses, or legal papers received in connection with a claim or suit. Argent Birch Employers will manage the legal response to such actions, utilizing appointed counsel to navigate the complexities of the litigation. The carrier retains the exclusive authority to investigate, negotiate, and settle any claim or suit as deemed appropriate.

Coverage under this section is subject to specific limitations regarding the maximum financial responsibility of the carrier. These limitations apply separately to bodily injury by accident, bodily injury by disease per employee, and an aggregate limit for bodily injury by disease. The application of the experience modification factor does not alter these established limitations.

Exclusions apply to liability assumed under a contract, punitive damages, and injuries sustained by employees employed in violation of the law with the actual knowledge of the named insured. Furthermore, this section does not apply to any obligation imposed by a workers compensation, occupational disease, unemployment compensation, or disability benefits law.

References to classification, remuneration, and rating basis include MA class code 5190 only for the state and operation shown in the information page.

Headings are included for ease of reading and do not alter statutory benefits, employers liability limits, audit rights, or state amendatory provisions.

If a state endorsement and a general condition address the same subject, the state-specific endorsement controls for the affected state.

The insured should retain payroll journals, tax filings, subcontractor certificates, job-duty records, and officer status records used to support the classification entries.

Classification summaries on one page do not replace the information page, payroll schedule, endorsement schedule, or premium audit statement.

A certificate, binder note, invoice, or producer correspondence item does not amend a payroll or class-code entry unless an endorsement is issued.

Final premium may require allocation of remuneration by state, governing class, officer status, overtime treatment, and subcontracted work records.

When a class code appears on multiple schedules, the state, item identifier, and effective date should be used to read the entries together.

SECTION A - RECORDS AND AUDIT

The insured must keep payroll journals, tax filings, job-duty records, and contract labor records for Electrical wiring within buildings assigned to class code 5190 in MA.

The remuneration entry of $77,560 is an estimate for rating purposes and may be revised after audit without changing the coverage afforded by the policy.

Separate records are required when an employee performs duties that may fall under more than one classification or more than one covered state.

If adequate records are not available, remuneration may be assigned to the highest rated applicable classification permitted by the rating rules.

SECTION B - STATE AND CLASSIFICATION CONDITIONS

State amendatory endorsements, statutory benefit provisions, and assigned-risk rules apply before any conflicting general condition in this policy packet.

A classification shown on a schedule is not a warranty that all operations at the insured location are limited to that class.

Officer, partner, member, volunteer, leased-worker, and subcontractor treatment is determined by the attached endorsements and the applicable state rules.

Certificates from subcontractors must be available for audit and must identify the period of work, covered operations, and limits carried by the subcontractor.

Blue Kettle Food Service, LLC                                                      WC 04 03 06

Massachusetts State Amendatory Endorsement                                    04/01/2026 - 04/01/2027

====================================================================================================
                             MASSACHUSETTS STATE AMENDATORY ENDORSEMENT
====================================================================================================

WC-MA-AMEND policy form                                                          Policy No. YW700400

"ITEM","STATE / CLASS"
"WC-0005","RI / 9082"
"CLASSIFICATION","PAYROLL / RATE"
"Restaurant NOC","$90,759 / 0.27"
"PREMIUM","FORM"
"$245","WC 00 00 01 A 01 15"

THIS AMENDATORY DOCUMENT MODIFIES THE ADMINISTRATIVE PROCEDURES FOR OPERATIONS CONDUCTED WITHIN THE COMMONWEALTH OF MASSACHUSETTS. THE PROVISIONS CONTAINED HEREIN SUPERSEDE ANY CONFLICTING LANGUAGE WITHIN THE GENERAL POLICY CONDITIONS. THIS ENDORSEMENT APPLIES SPECIFICALLY TO THE REMUNERATION AND OCCUPATIONAL HAZARDS ASSOCIATED WITH CLASS CODES 8742 AND 5190, AS SCHEDULED FOR THE MASSACHUSETTS LOCATIONS.

Any disputes regarding the assignment of classification codes, the calculation of estimated premium, or the application of the experience modification factor must be submitted to the Workers' Compensation Rating and Inspection Bureau of Massachusetts. Argent Birch Employers and Blue Kettle Food Service, LLC are bound by the determinations issued by the state rating bureau regarding these administrative matters.

The cancellation and nonrenewal provisions are amended to comply with Massachusetts statutory requirements. The carrier must provide written notice of cancellation to the named insured and the appropriate state agency within the mandated timeframes. The notice must clearly state the specific reasons for the cancellation, such as nonpayment of premium or a material misrepresentation of operational hazards.

Statutory benefits for occupational injuries sustained within Massachusetts will be administered strictly in accordance with Chapter 152 of the General Laws. The named insured must comply with all state-mandated reporting requirements, including the prompt submission of the Employer's First Report of Injury or Fatality for any incident resulting in lost time or medical treatment beyond first aid.

References to classification, remuneration, and rating basis include RI class code 9082 only for the state and operation shown in the information page.

Headings are included for ease of reading and do not alter statutory benefits, employers liability limits, audit rights, or state amendatory provisions.

If a state endorsement and a general condition address the same subject, the state-specific endorsement controls for the affected state.

The insured should retain payroll journals, tax filings, subcontractor certificates, job-duty records, and officer status records used to support the classification entries.

Classification summaries on one page do not replace the information page, payroll schedule, endorsement schedule, or premium audit statement.

A certificate, binder note, invoice, or producer correspondence item does not amend a payroll or class-code entry unless an endorsement is issued.

Final premium may require allocation of remuneration by state, governing class, officer status, overtime treatment, and subcontracted work records.

When a class code appears on multiple schedules, the state, item identifier, and effective date should be used to read the entries together.

SECTION A - RECORDS AND AUDIT

The insured must keep payroll journals, tax filings, job-duty records, and contract labor records for Restaurant NOC assigned to class code 9082 in RI.

The remuneration entry of $90,759 is an estimate for rating purposes and may be revised after audit without changing the coverage afforded by the policy.

Separate records are required when an employee performs duties that may fall under more than one classification or more than one covered state.

If adequate records are not available, remuneration may be assigned to the highest rated applicable classification permitted by the rating rules.

SECTION B - STATE AND CLASSIFICATION CONDITIONS

State amendatory endorsements, statutory benefit provisions, and assigned-risk rules apply before any conflicting general condition in this policy packet.

A classification shown on a schedule is not a warranty that all operations at the insured location are limited to that class.

Officer, partner, member, volunteer, leased-worker, and subcontractor treatment is determined by the attached endorsements and the applicable state rules.

Certificates from subcontractors must be available for audit and must identify the period of work, covered operations, and limits carried by the subcontractor.

Blue Kettle Food Service, LLC                                                            WC-MA-AMEND

| **EMPLOYERS LIABILITY PROVISIONS ADDRESS THE FINANCIAL CONSEQUENCES OF WORKPLACE INJURIES NOT STRICTLY RESOLVED THROUGH STATUTORY WORKERS COMPENSATION FRAMEWORKS. THIS SECTION APPLIES TO BODILY INJURY BY ACCIDENT OR BODILY INJURY BY DISEASE ARISING OUT OF AND IN THE COURSE OF THE INJURED EMPLOYEE'S EMPLOYMENT BY BLUE KETTLE FOOD SERVICE, LLC. THE INJURY MUST OCCUR DURING THE POLICY PERIOD AND WITHIN THE DESIGNATED COVERAGE TERRITORIES.**<br><br>The insured entity must immediately forward any demands, notices, summonses, or legal papers received in connection with a claim or suit. Argent Birch Employers will manage the legal response to such actions, utilizing appointed counsel to navigate the complexities of the litigation. The carrier retains the exclusive authority to investigate, negotiate, and settle any claim or suit as deemed appropriate.<br><br>Coverage under this section is subject to specific limitations regarding the maximum financial responsibility of the carrier. These limitations apply separately to bodily injury by accident, bodily injury by disease per employee, and an aggregate limit for bodily injury by disease. The application of the experience modification factor does not alter these established limitations.<br><br>Exclusions apply to liability assumed under a contract, punitive damages, and injuries sustained by employees employed in violation of the law with the actual knowledge of the named insured. Furthermore, this section does not apply to any obligation imposed by a workers compensation, occupational disease, unemployment compensation, or disability benefits law.<br><br>References to classification, remuneration, and rating basis include MA class code 8742 only for the state and operation shown in the information page.<br><br>Headings are included for ease of reading and do not alter statutory benefits, employers liability limits, audit rights, or state amendatory provisions.<br><br>If a state endorsement and a general condition address the same subject, the state-specific endorsement controls for the affected state. | The insured should retain payroll journals, tax filings, subcontractor certificates, job-duty records, and officer status records used to support the classification entries.<br><br>Classification summaries on one page do not replace the information page, payroll schedule, endorsement schedule, or premium audit statement.<br><br>A certificate, binder note, invoice, or producer correspondence item does not amend a payroll or class-code entry unless an endorsement is issued.<br><br>Final premium may require allocation of remuneration by state, governing class, officer status, overtime treatment, and subcontracted work records.<br><br>When a class code appears on multiple schedules, the state, item identifier, and effective date should be used to read the entries together.<br><br>**SECTION A - RECORDS AND AUDIT**<br><br>The insured must keep payroll journals, tax filings, job-duty records, and contract labor records for Outside salespersons assigned to class code 8742 in MA.<br><br>The remuneration entry of $256,691 is an estimate for rating purposes and may be revised after audit without changing the coverage afforded by the policy.<br><br>Separate records are required when an employee performs duties that may fall under more than one classification or more than one covered state.<br><br>If adequate records are not available, remuneration may be assigned to the highest rated applicable classification permitted by the rating rules.<br><br>**SECTION B - | **BRINDLE COAST COVERAGE GROUP, OPERATING UNDER PRODUCER CODE PX-73916, RECEIVES COMPENSATION FOR THE PLACEMENT AND SERVICING OF THIS POLICY. THIS DISCLOSURE OUTLINES THE NATURE OF THE FINANCIAL ARRANGEMENT BETWEEN ARGENT BIRCH EMPLOYERS AND THE DESIGNATED PRODUCER. THE COMPENSATION IS INCORPORATED INTO THE OVERALL PREMIUM STRUCTURE AND DOES NOT REPRESENT AN ADDITIONAL FEE CHARGED DIRECTLY TO THE NAMED INSURED.**<br><br>The compensation may include base commissions calculated as a percentage of the final audited premium. The commission rate varies depending on the line of business, the state of operation, and the specific contractual agreement between the carrier and the producer. The base commission compensates the producer for activities such as risk assessment, policy negotiation, and ongoing customer service.<br><br>In addition to base commissions, Brindle Coast Coverage Group may be eligible for contingent compensation based on the aggregate performance of a portfolio of policies placed with Argent Birch Employers. Contingent compensation is typically tied to metrics such as profitability, retention rates, and premium volume. This variable compensation is not guaranteed and is calculated retrospectively.<br><br>Blue Kettle Food Service, LLC may request detailed information regarding the specific compensation associated with policy number YW700400. Requests for detailed compensation disclosures must be submitted in writing to the carrier. | This document establishes the foundational parameters for workers compensation and employers liability coverage across multiple jurisdictions. | **THIS ENDORSEMENT ESTABLISHES A FRAMEWORK FOR PROVIDING STATUTORY BENEFITS TO INDIVIDUALS WHO MAY NOT FALL WITHIN THE MANDATORY SCOPE OF THE APPLICABLE STATE WORKERS COMPENSATION STATUTES. BLUE KETTLE FOOD SERVICE, LLC MAY ELECT TO OFFER THESE BENEFITS TO EXEMPT EMPLOYEES, INDEPENDENT CONTRACTORS, OR VOLUNTEERS, PROVIDED SUCH INDIVIDUALS SUSTAIN AN OCCUPATIONAL INJURY WHILE PERFORMING DUTIES DIRECTLY RELATED TO THE SCHEDULED OPERATIONS.** | The insured should retain payroll journals, tax filings, subcontractor certificates, job-duty records, and officer status records used to support the classification entries. <br><br> Classification summaries on one page do not replace the information page, payroll schedule, endorsement schedule, or premium audit statement. |
| The provision of voluntary benefits is contingent upon the injured individual executing a full release of liability in favor of the named insured and Argent Birch Employers. The injured party must waive any common law rights to pursue civil litigation regarding the workplace incident. If the individual rejects the voluntary benefits and initiates a civil action, the provisions of this endorsement immediately cease to apply to that specific incident. | A certificate, binder note, invoice, or producer correspondence item does not amend a payroll or class-code entry unless an endorsement is issued. <br><br> Final premium may require allocation of remuneration by state, governing class, officer status, overtime treatment, and subcontracted work records. <br><br> When a class code appears on multiple schedules, the state, item identifier, and effective date should be used to read the entries together. |
| Remuneration for individuals covered under this voluntary arrangement must be included in the payroll records and assigned to the classification code that most accurately reflects their occupational duties. The manual rates, experience modification factor, and schedule rating adjustments will be applied to this remuneration in the same manner as mandatory payroll. | **SECTION A - RECORDS AND AUDIT** <br><br> The insured must keep payroll journals, tax filings, job-duty records, and contract labor records for Building operations by owner assigned to class code 9015 in NH. <br><br> The remuneration entry of $296,731 is an estimate for rating purposes and may be revised after audit without changing the coverage afforded by the policy. |
| Argent Birch Employers will administer the voluntary benefits in accordance with the statutory schedules of the state where the injury occurred, as if the injured individual were a mandatory employee. THE ESTIMATED PREMIUM FOR POLICY NUMBER YW700400 TOTALS THE SUM OF THE INDIVIDUAL CLASS CODE ESTIMATES ACROSS ALL SCHEDULED STATES. THIS INITIAL FINANCIAL OBLIGATION IS BASED ON THE ANTICIPATED REMUNERATION PROVIDED BY BLUE KETTLE FOOD SERVICE, LLC. THE BILLING SCHEDULE DICTATES THE TIMING AND STRUCTURE OF THE PREMIUM INSTALLMENTS REQUIRED TO MAINTAIN THE COVERAGE IN FORCE DURING THE POLICY PERIOD.

For Connecticut operations, the initial billing incorporates the estimated premium of $189 for clerical operations and $400 for retail operations. Massachusetts operations contribute $127 for outside salespersons and $2,218 for electrical wiring activities. These base amounts are subject to the application of the 1.04 experience modification factor, which adjusts the total estimated premium upward.

The named insured may elect to remit the total estimated premium in a single annual payment or utilize an approved installment plan. If an installment plan is selected, the carrier will issue periodic invoices detailing the current amount due, the payment deadline, and any applicable installment fees. Failure to remit payment by the specified deadline may result in the initiation of cancellation procedures.

All premium payments must be directed to the designated lockbox or processed through the carrier's electronic payment portal. Brindle Coast Coverage Group is not authorized to accept premium payments on behalf of Argent Birch Employers unless specifically granted written authority. The final financial reconciliation will occur following the completion of the premium audit.

References to classification, remuneration, and rating basis include CT class code 8810 only for the state and operation shown in the information page.

Headings are included for ease of reading and do not alter statutory benefits, employers liability limits, audit rights, or state amendatory provisions.

If a state endorsement and a general condition address the same subject, the state-specific endorsement controls for the affected state.

The insured should retain payroll journals, tax filings, subcontractor certificates, job-duty records, and officer status records used to support the classification entries.

***

Classification summaries on one page do not replace the information page, payroll schedule, endorsement schedule, or premium audit statement.

A certificate, binder note, invoice, or producer correspondence item does not amend a payroll or class-code entry unless an endorsement is issued.

Final premium may require allocation of remuneration by state, governing class, officer status, overtime treatment, and subcontracted work records.

When a class code appears on multiple schedules, the state, item identifier, and effective date should be used to read the entries together.

SECTION A - RECORDS AND AUDIT

The insured must keep payroll journals, tax filings, job-duty records, and contract labor records for Clerical office employees assigned to class code 8810 in CT.

The remuneration entry of $323,486 is an estimate for rating purposes and may be revised after audit without changing the coverage afforded by the policy.

Separate records are required when an employee performs duties that may fall under more than one classification or more than one covered state.

If adequate records are not available, remuneration may be assigned to the highest rated applicable classification permitted by the rating rules.

SECTION B - STATE AND CLASSIFICATION CONDITIONS

State amendatory endorsements, statutory benefit provisions, and assigned-risk rules apply before any conflicting general condition in this policy packet.

A classification shown on a schedule is not a warranty that all operations at the insured location are limited to that class.

Officer, partner, member, volunteer, leased-worker, and subcontractor treatment is determined by the attached endorsements and the applicable state rules.

Certificates from subcontractors must be available for audit and must identify the period of work, covered operations, and limits carried by the subcontractor.

ITEM,STATE / CLASS

ARGENT BIRCH EMPLOYERS REQUIRES THE MAINTENANCE OF PRECISE PAYROLL RECORDS FOR ALL INDIVIDUALS ENGAGED BY BLUE KETTLE FOOD SERVICE, LLC. THIS NOTIFICATION SERVES AS A FORMAL REMINDER OF THE RECORDKEEPING OBLIGATIONS ESSENTIAL FOR THE FINAL PREMIUM DETERMINATION. ACCURATE DOCUMENTATION IS CRITICAL FOR THE PROPER ASSIGNMENT OF REMUNERATION TO THE SCHEDULED CLASSIFICATION CODES, INCLUDING 8810, 8017, 8742, AND 5190.

The required documentation includes, but is not limited to, state and federal tax summaries, individual employee earnings records, general ledgers, cash disbursement journals, and certificates of insurance for all independent contractors utilized during the policy period. The records must clearly indicate the specific duties performed by each individual and the state in which those duties were executed.

Particular attention must be given to the segregation of payroll for employees who perform duties that span multiple classification codes. The named insured must maintain verifiable daily time records detailing the hours dedicated to each specific occupational task. In the absence of such detailed records, the entire remuneration for the employee will be assigned to the highest-rated classification code applicable to their duties.

Failure to provide adequate documentation during the final audit may result in the application of penalty provisions, including the assignment of undocumented remuneration to the highest-rated classification code or the implementation of an audit noncompliance charge. The named insured must ensure that all relevant records are readily accessible for review by the carrier's audit personnel.

References to classification, remuneration, and rating basis include RI class code 9082 only for the state and operation shown in the information page.

Headings are included for ease of reading and do not alter statutory benefits, employers liability limits, audit rights, or state amendatory provisions.

If a state endorsement and a general condition address the same subject, the state-specific endorsement controls for the affected state.

The insured should retain payroll journals, tax filings, subcontractor certificates, job-duty records, and officer status records used to support the classification entries.

Classification summaries on one page do not replace the information page, payroll schedule, endorsement schedule, or premium audit statement.

A certificate, binder note, invoice, or producer correspondence item does not amend a payroll or class-code entry unless an endorsement is issued.

Final premium may require allocation of remuneration by state, governing class, officer status, overtime treatment, and subcontracted work records.

When a class code appears on multiple schedules, the state, item identifier, and effective date should be used to read the entries together.

SECTION A - RECORDS AND AUDIT
The insured must keep payroll journals, tax filings, job-duty records, and contract labor records for Restaurant NOC assigned to class code 9082 in RI.

The remuneration entry of $90,759 is an estimate for rating purposes and may be revised after audit without changing the coverage afforded by the policy.

Separate records are required when an employee performs duties that may fall under more than one classification or more than one covered state.

If adequate records are not available, remuneration may be assigned to the highest rated applicable classification permitted by the rating rules.

SECTION B - STATE AND CLASSIFICATION CONDITIONS
State amendatory endorsements, statutory benefit provisions, and assigned-risk rules apply before any conflicting general condition in this policy packet.

A classification shown on a schedule is not a warranty that all operations at the insured location are limited to that class.

Officer, partner, member, volunteer, leased-worker, and subcontractor treatment is determined by the attached endorsements and the applicable state rules.

Certificates from subcontractors must be available for audit and must identify the period of work, covered operations, and limits carried by the subcontractor.

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Blue Kettle Food Service, LLC                                                                WC-NT-02

                                VOLUNTARY COMPENSATION ENDORSEMENT
====================================================================================================

WC 00 00 00 C policy form                                                            Policy No. YW700400

ITEM,STATE / CLASS
WC-0008,VT / 5606
CLASSIFICATION,PAYROLL / RATE
Contractor executive supervisor,$127,460 / 6.22
PREMIUM,FORM
$7,928,WC 00 00 01 A 04 21

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

THIS ENDORSEMENT ESTABLISHES A FRAMEWORK FOR PROVIDING STATUTORY BENEFITS TO INDIVIDUALS WHO MAY NOT FALL WITHIN THE MANDATORY SCOPE OF THE APPLICABLE STATE WORKERS COMPENSATION STATUTES. BLUE KETTLE FOOD SERVICE, LLC MAY ELECT TO OFFER THESE BENEFITS TO EXEMPT EMPLOYEES, INDEPENDENT CONTRACTORS, OR VOLUNTEERS, PROVIDED SUCH INDIVIDUALS SUSTAIN AN OCCUPATIONAL INJURY WHILE PERFORMING DUTIES DIRECTLY RELATED TO THE SCHEDULED OPERATIONS.

The provision of voluntary benefits is contingent upon the injured individual executing a full release of liability in favor of the named insured and Argent Birch Employers. The injured party must waive any common law rights to pursue civil litigation regarding the workplace incident. If the individual rejects the voluntary benefits and initiates a civil action, the provisions of this endorsement immediately cease to apply to that specific incident.

Remuneration for individuals covered under this voluntary arrangement must be included in the payroll records and assigned to the classification code that most accurately reflects their occupational duties. The manual rates, experience modification factor, and schedule rating adjustments will be applied to this remuneration in the same manner as mandatory payroll.

Argent Birch Employers will administer the voluntary benefits in accordance with the statutory schedules of the state where the injury occurred, as if the injured individual were a mandatory employee. The named insured must promptly notify the carrier of any injury involving a voluntarily covered individual and facilitate the execution of the required release documents.

References to classification, remuneration, and rating basis include VT class code 5606 only for the state and operation shown in the information page.

Headings are included for ease of reading and do not alter statutory benefits, employers liability limits, audit rights, or state amendatory provisions.

If a state endorsement and a general condition address the same subject, the state-specific endorsement controls for the affected state.

The insured should retain payroll journals, tax filings, subcontractor certificates, job-duty records, and officer status records used to support the classification entries.

Classification summaries on one page do not replace the information page, payroll schedule, endorsement schedule, or premium audit statement.

A certificate, binder note, invoice, or producer correspondence item does not amend a payroll or class-code entry unless an endorsement is issued.

Final premium may require allocation of remuneration by state, governing class, officer status, overtime treatment, and subcontracted work records.

When a class code appears on multiple schedules, the state, item identifier, and effective date should be used to read the entries together.

SECTION A - RECORDS AND AUDIT

The insured must keep payroll journals, tax filings, job-duty records, and contract labor records for Contractor executive supervisor assigned to class code 5606 in VT.

The remuneration entry of $127,460 is an estimate for rating purposes and may be revised after audit without changing the coverage afforded by the policy.

Separate records are required when an employee performs duties that may fall under more than one classification or more than one covered state.

If adequate records are not available, remuneration may be assigned to the highest rated applicable classification permitted by the rating rules.

SECTION B - STATE AND CLASSIFICATION CONDITIONS

State amendatory endorsements, statutory benefit provisions, and assigned-risk rules apply before any conflicting general condition in this policy packet.

A classification shown on a schedule is not a warranty that all operations at the insured location are limited to that class.

Officer, partner, member, volunteer, leased-worker, and subcontractor treatment is determined by the attached endorsements and the applicable state rules.

Certificates from subcontractors must be available for audit and must identify the period of work, covered operations, and limits carried by the subcontractor.

In the absence of such detailed records, the entire remuneration for the employee will be assigned to the highest-rated classification code applicable to their duties. <br><br> Failure to provide adequate documentation during the final audit may result in the application of penalty provisions, including the assignment of undocumented remuneration to the highest-rated classification code or the implementation of an audit noncompliance charge. The named insured must ensure that all relevant records are readily accessible for review by the carrier's audit personnel. <br><br> References to classification, remuneration, and rating basis include CT class code 8810 only for the state and operation shown in the information page. <br><br> Headings are included for ease of reading and do not alter statutory benefits, employers liability limits, audit rights, or state amendatory provisions. <br><br> If a state endorsement and a general condition address the same subject, the state-specific endorsement controls for the affected state. | The insured should retain payroll journals, tax filings, subcontractor certificates, job-duty records, and officer status records used to support the classification entries. <br><br> Classification summaries on one page do not replace the information page, payroll schedule, endorsement schedule, or premium audit statement. <br><br> A certificate, binder note, invoice, or producer correspondence item does not amend a payroll or class-code entry unless an endorsement is issued. <br><br> Final premium may require allocation of remuneration by state, governing class, officer status, overtime treatment, and subcontracted work records. <br><br> When a class code appears on multiple schedules, the state, item identifier, and effective date should be used to read the entries together. <br><br> **SECTION A - RECORDS AND AUDIT** <br><br> The insured must keep payroll journals, tax filings, job-duty records, and contract labor records for Clerical office employees assigned to class code 8810 in CT. <br><br> The remuneration entry of $139,137 is an estimate for rating purposes and may be revised after audit without changing the coverage afforded by the policy. <br><br> Separate records are required when an employee performs duties that may fall under more than one classification or more than one covered state. <br><br> If adequate records are not available, remuneration may be assigned to the highest rated applicable classification permitted by the rating rules. <br><br> **SECTION B - --------------------------------------------------------------------------------

ARGENT BIRCH EMPLOYERS PROVIDES THE COVERAGE DETAILED HEREIN TO THE NAMED INSURED, BLUE KETTLE FOOD SERVICE, LLC, WHOSE PRIMARY MAILING ADDRESS IS RECORDED AS 914 MILLRACE PARKWAY, WORCESTER, MA 01608. THE ADMINISTRATIVE PARAMETERS OF THIS CONTRACT ARE GOVERNED BY THE DECLARATIONS AND THE CORRESPONDING STATE-SPECIFIC SCHEDULES ATTACHED AT ISSUANCE. THE POLICY PERIOD COMMENCES ON 04/01/2026 AND CONCLUDES ON 04/01/2027, WITH ALL EFFECTIVE DATES BEGINNING AT STANDARD TIME AT THE PRIMARY MAILING ADDRESS OF THE NAMED INSURED.

This document establishes the foundational parameters for workers compensation and employers liability coverage across multiple jurisdictions. Operations are currently scheduled for the states of Connecticut and Massachusetts. The classification schedule assigns estimated remuneration to the states and class codes shown. Final premium may change if payroll records, job duties, or state assignments differ from the estimates used at issuance.

The experience modification factor of 1.04 and the schedule rating adjustment of 0% apply to the policy as a whole unless a state-specific endorsement provides otherwise. These rating elements are applied to the manual premium generated by the audited payroll to determine the final financial obligation of the named insured. Brindle Coast Coverage Group, operating under producer code PX-73916, serves as the designated representative for this transaction.

The employer must maintain detailed ledgers segregating remuneration by state and classification code. Argent Birch Employers retains the authority to examine and audit all financial records, tax documents, and employment contracts associated with Blue Kettle Food Service, LLC during the policy period and within three years following its expiration.

References to classification, remuneration, and rating basis include MA class code 8742 only for the state and operation shown in the information page.

Headings are included for ease of reading and do not alter statutory benefits, employers liability limits, audit rights, or state amendatory provisions.

If a state endorsement and a general condition address the same subject, the state-specific endorsement controls for the affected state.

The insured should retain payroll journals, tax filings, subcontractor certificates, job-duty records, and officer status records used to support the classification entries.

Classification summaries on one page do not replace the information page, payroll schedule, endorsement schedule, or premium audit statement.

A certificate, binder note, invoice, or producer correspondence item does not amend a payroll or class-code entry unless an endorsement is issued.

Final premium may require allocation of remuneration by state, governing class, officer status, overtime treatment, and subcontracted work records.

When a class code appears on multiple schedules, the state, item identifier, and effective date should be used to read the entries together.

SECTION A - RECORDS AND AUDIT

The insured must keep payroll journals, tax filings, job-duty records, and contract labor records for Outside salespersons assigned to class code 8742 in MA.

The remuneration entry of $158,051 is an estimate for rating purposes and may be revised after audit without changing the coverage afforded by the policy.

Separate records are required when an employee performs duties that may fall under more than one classification or more than one covered state.

If adequate records are not available, remuneration may be assigned to the highest rated applicable classification permitted by the rating rules.

SECTION B - STATE AND CLASSIFICATION CONDITIONS

State amendatory endorsements, statutory benefit provisions, and assigned-risk rules apply before any conflicting general condition in this policy packet.

A classification shown on a schedule is not a warranty that all operations at the insured location are limited to that class.

Officer, partner, member, volunteer, leased-worker, and subcontractor treatment is determined by the attached endorsements and the applicable state rules.

Certificates from subcontractors must be available for audit and must identify the period of work, covered operations, and limits carried by the subcontractor.

Machine shop NOC,$195,887 / 6.22

EMPLOYERS LIABILITY PROVISIONS ADDRESS THE FINANCIAL CONSEQUENCES OF WORKPLACE INJURIES NOT STRICTLY RESOLVED THROUGH STATUTORY WORKERS COMPENSATION FRAMEWORKS. THIS SECTION APPLIES TO BODILY INJURY BY ACCIDENT OR BODILY INJURY BY DISEASE ARISING OUT OF AND IN THE COURSE OF THE INJURED EMPLOYEE'S EMPLOYMENT BY BLUE KETTLE FOOD SERVICE, LLC. THE INJURY MUST OCCUR DURING THE POLICY PERIOD AND WITHIN THE DESIGNATED COVERAGE TERRITORIES.

The insured entity must immediately forward any demands, notices, summonses, or legal papers received in connection with a claim or suit. Argent Birch Employers will manage the legal response to such actions, utilizing appointed counsel to navigate the complexities of the litigation. The carrier retains the exclusive authority to investigate, negotiate, and settle any claim or suit as deemed appropriate.

Coverage under this section is subject to specific limitations regarding the maximum financial responsibility of the carrier. These limitations apply separately to bodily injury by accident, bodily injury by disease per employee, and an aggregate limit for bodily injury by disease. The application of the experience modification factor does not alter these established limitations.

Exclusions apply to liability assumed under a contract, punitive damages, and injuries sustained by employees employed in violation of the law with the actual knowledge of the named insured. Furthermore, this section does not apply to any obligation imposed by a workers compensation, occupational disease, unemployment compensation, or disability benefits law.

References to classification, remuneration, and rating basis include ME class code 3632 only for the state and operation shown in the information page.

Headings are included for ease of reading and do not alter statutory benefits, employers liability limits, audit rights, or state amendatory provisions.

If a state endorsement and a general condition address the same subject, the state-specific endorsement controls for the affected state.

The insured should retain payroll journals, tax filings, subcontractor certificates, job-duty records, and officer status records used to support the classification entries.

Classification summaries on one page do not replace the information page, payroll schedule, endorsement schedule, or premium audit statement.

A certificate, binder note, invoice, or producer correspondence item does not amend a payroll or class-code entry unless an endorsement is issued.

Final premium may require allocation of remuneration by state, governing class, officer status, overtime treatment, and subcontracted work records.

When a class code appears on multiple schedules, the state, item identifier, and effective date should be used to read the entries together.

SECTION A - RECORDS AND AUDIT

The insured must keep payroll journals, tax filings, job-duty records, and contract labor records for Machine shop NOC assigned to class code 3632 in ME.

The remuneration entry of $195,887 is an estimate for rating purposes and may be revised after audit without changing the coverage afforded by the policy.

Separate records are required when an employee performs duties that may fall under more than one classification or more than one covered state.

If adequate records are not available, remuneration may be assigned to the highest rated applicable classification permitted by the rating rules.

SECTION B - STATE AND CLASSIFICATION CONDITIONS

State amendatory endorsements, statutory benefit provisions, and assigned-risk rules apply before any conflicting general condition in this policy packet.

A classification shown on a schedule is not a warranty that all operations at the insured location are limited to that class.

Officer, partner, member, volunteer, leased-worker, and subcontractor treatment is determined by the attached endorsements and the applicable state rules.

Certificates from subcontractors must be available for audit and must identify the period of work, covered operations, and limits carried by the subcontractor.

                           VOLUNTARY COMPENSATION ENDORSEMENT

WC 00 00 00 C policy form                                                        Policy No. YW700400

ITEM,STATE / CLASS
WC-0018,CT / 8017
CLASSIFICATION,PAYROLL / RATE
Retail store - all employees,$239,729 / 2.86
PREMIUM,FORM
$6,856,WC 00 00 00 C 04 21

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

THIS ENDORSEMENT ESTABLISHES A FRAMEWORK FOR PROVIDING STATUTORY BENEFITS TO INDIVIDUALS WHO MAY NOT FALL WITHIN THE MANDATORY SCOPE OF THE APPLICABLE STATE WORKERS COMPENSATION STATUTES. BLUE KETTLE FOOD SERVICE, LLC MAY ELECT TO OFFER THESE BENEFITS TO EXEMPT EMPLOYEES, INDEPENDENT CONTRACTORS, OR VOLUNTEERS, PROVIDED SUCH INDIVIDUALS SUSTAIN AN OCCUPATIONAL INJURY WHILE PERFORMING DUTIES DIRECTLY RELATED TO THE SCHEDULED OPERATIONS.

The provision of voluntary benefits is contingent upon the injured individual executing a full release of liability in favor of the named insured and Argent Birch Employers. The injured party must waive any common law rights to pursue civil litigation regarding the workplace incident. If the individual rejects the voluntary benefits and initiates a civil action, the provisions of this endorsement immediately cease to apply to that specific incident.

Remuneration for individuals covered under this voluntary arrangement must be included in the payroll records and assigned to the classification code that most accurately reflects their occupational duties. The manual rates, experience modification factor, and schedule rating adjustments will be applied to this remuneration in the same manner as mandatory payroll.

Argent Birch Employers will administer the voluntary benefits in accordance with the statutory schedules of the state where the injury occurred, as if the injured individual were a mandatory employee. The named insured must promptly notify the carrier of any injury involving a voluntarily covered individual and facilitate the execution of the required release documents.

References to classification, remuneration, and rating basis include CT class code 8017 only for the state and operation shown in the information page.

Headings are included for ease of reading and do not alter statutory benefits, employers liability limits, audit rights, or state amendatory provisions.

If a state endorsement and a general condition address the same subject, the state-specific endorsement controls for the affected state.

The insured should retain payroll journals, tax filings, subcontractor certificates, job-duty records, and officer status records used to support the classification entries.

Classification summaries on one page do not replace the information page, payroll schedule, endorsement schedule, or premium audit statement.

A certificate, binder note, invoice, or producer correspondence item does not amend a payroll or class-code entry unless an endorsement is issued.

Final premium may require allocation of remuneration by state, governing class, officer status, overtime treatment, and subcontracted work records.

When a class code appears on multiple schedules, the state, item identifier, and effective date should be used to read the entries together.

SECTION A - RECORDS AND AUDIT
The insured must keep payroll journals, tax filings, job-duty records, and contract labor records for Retail store - all employees assigned to class code 8017 in CT.

The remuneration entry of $239,729 is an estimate for rating purposes and may be revised after audit without changing the coverage afforded by the policy.

Separate records are required when an employee performs duties that may fall under more than one classification or more than one covered state.

If adequate records are not available, remuneration may be assigned to the highest rated applicable classification permitted by the rating rules.

SECTION B - STATE AND CLASSIFICATION CONDITIONS
State amendatory endorsements, statutory benefit provisions, and assigned-risk rules apply before any conflicting general condition in this policy packet.

A classification shown on a schedule is not a warranty that all operations at the insured location are limited to that class.

Officer, partner, member, volunteer, leased-worker, and subcontractor treatment is determined by the attached endorsements and the applicable state rules.

Certificates from subcontractors must be available for audit and must identify the period of work, covered operations, and limits carried by the subcontractor.

Blue Kettle Food Service, LLC                                                    WC 00 00 00 C

**Outside salespersons**                                     **$70,826 / 0.18**

PREMIUM                                                      FORM
**$127**                                                     **WC 00 00 00 C 01 15**
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

=======================================================================================================
[COLUMN 1]

**THIS ENDORSEMENT ESTABLISHES A FRAMEWORK FOR PROVIDING STATUTORY BENEFITS TO INDIVIDUALS WHO MAY NOT FALL WITHIN THE MANDATORY SCOPE OF THE APPLICABLE STATE WORKERS COMPENSATION STATUTES. BLUE KETTLE FOOD SERVICE, LLC MAY ELECT TO OFFER THESE BENEFITS TO EXEMPT EMPLOYEES, INDEPENDENT CONTRACTORS, OR VOLUNTEERS, PROVIDED SUCH INDIVIDUALS SUSTAIN AN OCCUPATIONAL INJURY WHILE PERFORMING DUTIES DIRECTLY RELATED TO THE SCHEDULED OPERATIONS.**

The provision of voluntary benefits is contingent upon the injured individual executing a full release of liability in favor of the named insured and Argent Birch Employers. The injured party must waive any common law rights to pursue civil litigation regarding the workplace incident. If the individual rejects the voluntary benefits and initiates a civil action, the provisions of this endorsement immediately cease to apply to that specific incident.

Remuneration for individuals covered under this voluntary arrangement must be included in the payroll records and assigned to the classification code that most accurately reflects their occupational duties. The manual rates, experience modification factor, and schedule rating adjustments will be applied to this remuneration in the same manner as mandatory payroll.

Argent Birch Employers will administer the voluntary benefits in accordance with the statutory schedules of the state where the injury occurred, as if the injured individual were a mandatory employee. The named insured must promptly notify the carrier of any injury involving a voluntarily covered individual and facilitate the execution of the required release documents.

References to classification, remuneration, and rating basis include MA class code 8742 only for the state and operation shown in the information page.

Headings are included for ease of reading and do not alter statutory benefits, employers liability limits, audit rights, or state amendatory provisions.

If a state endorsement and a general condition address the same subject, the state-specific endorsement controls for the affected state.

=======================================================================================================
[COLUMN 2]

The insured should retain payroll journals, tax filings, subcontractor certificates, job-duty records, and officer status records used to support the classification entries.

Classification summaries on one page do not replace the information page, payroll schedule, endorsement schedule, or premium audit statement.

A certificate, binder note, invoice, or producer correspondence item does not amend a payroll or class-code entry unless an endorsement is issued.

Final premium may require allocation of remuneration by state, governing class, officer status, overtime treatment, and subcontracted work records.

When a class code appears on multiple schedules, the state, item identifier, and effective date should be used to read the entries together.

**SECTION A - RECORDS AND AUDIT**

The insured must keep payroll journals, tax filings, job-duty records, and contract labor records for Outside salespersons assigned to class code 8742 in MA.

The remuneration entry of $70,826 is an estimate for rating purposes and may be revised after audit without changing the coverage afforded by the policy.

Separate records are required when an employee performs duties that may fall under more than one classification or more than one covered state.

If adequate records are not available, remuneration may be assigned to the highest rated applicable classification permitted by the rating rules.

**SECTION B - STATE AND CLASSIFICATION CONDITIONS**

State amendatory endorsements, statutory benefit provisions, and assigned-risk rules apply before any conflicting general condition in this policy packet.

A classification shown on a schedule is not a warranty that all operations at the insured location are limited to that class.

Officer, partner, member, volunteer, leased-worker, and subcontractor treatment is determined by the attached endorsements and the applicable state rules.

Certificates from subcontractors must be available for audit and must identify the period of work, covered operations, and limits carried by the subcontractor.

Failure to remit payment by the specified deadline may result in the initiation of cancellation procedures.

All premium payments must be directed to the designated lockbox or processed through the carrier's electronic payment portal. Brindle Coast Coverage Group is not authorized to accept premium payments on behalf of Argent Birch Employers unless specifically granted written authority. The final financial reconciliation will occur following the completion of the premium audit.

BRINDLE COAST COVERAGE GROUP, OPERATING UNDER PRODUCER CODE PX-73916, RECEIVES COMPENSATION FOR THE PLACEMENT AND SERVICING OF THIS POLICY. THIS DISCLOSURE OUTLINES THE NATURE OF THE FINANCIAL ARRANGEMENT BETWEEN ARGENT BIRCH EMPLOYERS AND THE DESIGNATED PRODUCER. THE COMPENSATION IS INCORPORATED INTO THE OVERALL PREMIUM STRUCTURE AND DOES NOT REPRESENT AN ADDITIONAL FEE CHARGED DIRECTLY TO THE NAMED INSURED.

The compensation may include base commissions calculated as a percentage of the final audited premium. The commission rate varies depending on the line of business, the state of operation, and the specific contractual agreement between the carrier and the producer. The base commission compensates the producer for activities such as risk assessment, policy negotiation, and ongoing customer service.

In addition to base commissions, Brindle Coast Coverage Group may be eligible for contingent compensation based on the aggregate performance of a portfolio of policies placed with Argent Birch Employers. Contingent compensation is typically tied to metrics such as profitability, retention rates, and premium volume. This variable compensation is not guaranteed and is calculated retrospectively.

Blue Kettle Food Service, LLC may request detailed information regarding the specific compensation associated with policy number YW700400. Requests for detailed compensation disclosures must be submitted in writing to the carrier. Argent Birch Employers is committed to maintaining transparency regarding producer compensation arrangements.

References to classification, remuneration, and rating basis include ME class code 3632 only for the state and operation shown in the information page.

Headings are included for ease of reading and do not alter statutory benefits, employers liability limits, audit rights, or state amendatory provisions.

If a state endorsement and a general condition address the same subject, the state-specific endorsement controls for the affected state.

The insured should retain payroll journals, tax filings, subcontractor certificates, job-duty records, and officer status records used to support the classification entries.


Classification summaries on one page do not replace the information page, payroll schedule, endorsement schedule, or premium audit statement.

A certificate, binder note, invoice, or producer correspondence item does not amend a payroll or class-code entry unless an endorsement is issued.

Final premium may require allocation of remuneration by state, governing class, officer status, overtime treatment, and subcontracted work records.

When a class code appears on multiple schedules, the state, item identifier, and effective date should be used to read the entries together.

SECTION A - RECORDS AND AUDIT

The insured must keep payroll journals, tax filings, job-duty records, and contract labor records for Machine shop NOC assigned to class code 3632 in ME.

The remuneration entry of $195,887 is an estimate for rating purposes and may be revised after audit without changing the coverage afforded by the policy.

Separate records are required when an employee performs duties that may fall under more than one classification or more than one covered state.

If adequate records are not available, remuneration may be assigned to the highest rated applicable classification permitted by the rating rules.

SECTION B - STATE AND CLASSIFICATION CONDITIONS

State amendatory endorsements, statutory benefit provisions, and assigned-risk rules apply before any conflicting general condition in this policy packet.

A classification shown on a schedule is not a warranty that all operations at the insured location are limited to that class.

Officer, partner, member, volunteer, leased-worker, and subcontractor treatment is determined by the attached endorsements and the applicable state rules.

Certificates from subcontractors must be available for audit and must identify the period of work, covered operations, and limits carried by the subcontractor.

WC 00 00 00 C policy form                                             Policy No. YW700400

ITEM,STATE / CLASS
WC-0023,NH / 9015
CLASSIFICATION,PAYROLL / RATE
Building operations by owner,$296,731 / 0.74
PREMIUM,FORM
$2,195,WC 04 03 06 04 21

THIS ENDORSEMENT ESTABLISHES A FRAMEWORK FOR PROVIDING STATUTORY BENEFITS TO INDIVIDUALS WHO MAY NOT FALL WITHIN THE MANDATORY SCOPE OF THE APPLICABLE STATE WORKERS COMPENSATION STATUTES. BLUE KETTLE FOOD SERVICE, LLC MAY ELECT TO OFFER THESE BENEFITS TO EXEMPT EMPLOYEES, INDEPENDENT CONTRACTORS, OR VOLUNTEERS, PROVIDED SUCH INDIVIDUALS SUSTAIN AN OCCUPATIONAL INJURY WHILE PERFORMING DUTIES DIRECTLY RELATED TO THE SCHEDULED OPERATIONS.

The provision of voluntary benefits is contingent upon the injured individual executing a full release of liability in favor of the named insured and Argent Birch Employers. The injured party must waive any common law rights to pursue civil litigation regarding the workplace incident. If the individual rejects the voluntary benefits and initiates a civil action, the provisions of this endorsement immediately cease to apply to that specific incident.

Remuneration for individuals covered under this voluntary arrangement must be included in the payroll records and assigned to the classification code that most accurately reflects their occupational duties. The manual rates, experience modification factor, and schedule rating adjustments will be applied to this remuneration in the same manner as mandatory payroll.

Argent Birch Employers will administer the voluntary benefits in accordance with the statutory schedules of the state where the injury occurred, as if the injured individual were a mandatory employee. The named insured must promptly notify the carrier of any injury involving a voluntarily covered individual and facilitate the execution of the required release documents.

References to classification, remuneration, and rating basis include NH class code 9015 only for the state and operation shown in the information page.

Headings are included for ease of reading and do not alter statutory benefits, employers liability limits, audit rights, or state amendatory provisions.

If a state endorsement and a general condition address the same subject, the state-specific endorsement controls for the affected state.

The insured should retain payroll journals, tax filings, subcontractor certificates, job-duty records, and officer status records used to support the classification entries.

Classification summaries on one page do not replace the information page, payroll schedule, endorsement schedule, or premium audit statement.

A certificate, binder note, invoice, or producer correspondence item does not amend a payroll or class-code entry unless an endorsement is issued.

Final premium may require allocation of remuneration by state, governing class, officer status, overtime treatment, and subcontracted work records.

When a class code appears on multiple schedules, the state, item identifier, and effective date should be used to read the entries together.

SECTION A - RECORDS AND AUDIT

The insured must keep payroll journals, tax filings, job-duty records, and contract labor records for Building operations by owner assigned to class code 9015 in NH.

The remuneration entry of $296,731 is an estimate for rating purposes and may be revised after audit without changing the coverage afforded by the policy.

Separate records are required when an employee performs duties that may fall under more than one classification or more than one covered state.

If adequate records are not available, remuneration may be assigned to the highest rated applicable classification permitted by the rating rules.

SECTION B - STATE AND CLASSIFICATION CONDITIONS

State amendatory endorsements, statutory benefit provisions, and assigned-risk rules apply before any conflicting general condition in this policy packet.

A classification shown on a schedule is not a warranty that all operations at the insured location are limited to that class.

Officer, partner, member, volunteer, leased-worker, and subcontractor treatment is determined by the attached endorsements and the applicable state rules.

Certificates from subcontractors must be available for audit and must identify the period of work, covered operations, and limits carried by the subcontractor.

These rating elements are applied to the manual premium generated by the audited payroll to determine the final financial obligation of the named insured. PREMIUM AND PAYROLL AUDIT CONDITIONS

WC 00 04 10 policy form
Policy No. YW700400

ITEM,STATE / CLASS
WC-0010,CT / 8017
CLASSIFICATION,PAYROLL / RATE
Retail store - all employees,$152,897 / 4.35
PREMIUM,FORM
$6,651,WC 04 03 06 04 21

THE PREMIUM AMOUNTS DISPLAYED ON THE CLASSIFICATION SCHEDULE ARE ESTIMATES BASED ON THE ANTICIPATED PAYROLL FIGURES PROVIDED BY BLUE KETTLE FOOD SERVICE, LLC. THE FINAL PREMIUM CALCULATION REQUIRES A COMPREHENSIVE RETROSPECTIVE REVIEW OF ACTUAL REMUNERATION DISTRIBUTED DURING THE POLICY PERIOD. THIS AUDIT PROCESS ENSURES THAT THE PREMIUM ACCURATELY REFLECTS THE TRUE OCCUPATIONAL EXPOSURE ASSOCIATED WITH THE OPERATIONS IN CONNECTICUT AND MASSACHUSETTS.

The named insured is obligated to maintain meticulous financial records, including payroll ledgers, tax filings, and subcontractor invoices. These records must clearly segregate remuneration by individual employee, state of operation, and classification code. Failure to maintain adequate segregation may result in the entire payroll being assigned to the highest-rated classification code applicable to the employer's operations.

Argent Birch Employers will conduct the premium audit within a reasonable timeframe following the expiration or cancellation of the policy. The audit may be performed through a physical examination of records at the insured's premises, located at 914 Millrace Parkway, Worcester, MA 01608, or via a remote documentation review. The insured must cooperate fully with the designated audit personnel.

If the final audited premium exceeds the estimated premium paid during the policy period, the named insured will be billed for the additional amount. Conversely, if the audited premium is less than the estimated premium, the carrier will issue a refund or apply the credit to subsequent policy periods. The experience modification factor of 1.04 and the schedule rating adjustment of 0% will be applied to the final audited manual premium.

References to classification, remuneration, and rating basis include CT class code 8017 only for the state and operation shown in the information page.

Headings are included for ease of reading and do not alter statutory benefits, employers liability limits, audit rights, or state amendatory provisions.

If a state endorsement and a general condition address the same subject, the state-specific endorsement controls for the affected state.

The insured should retain payroll journals, tax filings, subcontractor certificates, job-duty records, and officer status records used to support the classification entries.

Classification summaries on one page do not replace the information page, payroll schedule, endorsement schedule, or premium audit statement.

A certificate, binder note, invoice, or producer correspondence item does not amend a payroll or class-code entry unless an endorsement is issued.

Final premium may require allocation of remuneration by state, governing class, officer status, overtime treatment, and subcontracted work records.

When a class code appears on multiple schedules, the state, item identifier, and effective date should be used to read the entries together.

SECTION A - RECORDS AND AUDIT

The insured must keep payroll journals, tax filings, job-duty records, and contract labor records for Retail store - all employees assigned to class code 8017 in CT.

The remuneration entry of $152,897 is an estimate for rating purposes and may be revised after audit without changing the coverage afforded by the policy.

Separate records are required when an employee performs duties that may fall under more than one classification or more than one covered state.

If adequate records are not available, remuneration may be assigned to the highest rated applicable classification permitted by the rating rules.

SECTION B - STATE AND CLASSIFICATION CONDITIONS

State amendatory endorsements, statutory benefit provisions, and assigned-risk rules apply before any conflicting general condition in this policy packet.

A classification shown on a schedule is not a warranty that all operations at the insured location are limited to that class.

Officer, partner, member, volunteer, leased-worker, and subcontractor treatment is determined by the attached endorsements and the applicable state rules.

Certificates from subcontractors must be available for audit and must identify the period of work, covered operations, and limits carried by the subcontractor.

____________________________________________________________________________________________________

**THE PREMIUM AMOUNTS DISPLAYED ON THE CLASSIFICATION SCHEDULE ARE ESTIMATES BASED ON THE ANTICIPATED PAYROLL FIGURES PROVIDED BY BLUE KETTLE FOOD SERVICE, LLC. THE FINAL PREMIUM CALCULATION REQUIRES A COMPREHENSIVE RETROSPECTIVE REVIEW OF ACTUAL REMUNERATION DISTRIBUTED DURING THE POLICY PERIOD. THIS AUDIT PROCESS ENSURES THAT THE PREMIUM ACCURATELY REFLECTS THE TRUE OCCUPATIONAL EXPOSURE ASSOCIATED WITH THE OPERATIONS IN CONNECTICUT AND MASSACHUSETTS.**

The named insured is obligated to maintain meticulous financial records, including payroll ledgers, tax filings, and subcontractor invoices. These records must clearly segregate remuneration by individual employee, state of operation, and classification code. Failure to maintain adequate segregation may result in the entire payroll being assigned to the highest-rated classification code applicable to the employer's operations.

Argent Birch Employers will conduct the premium audit within a reasonable timeframe following the expiration or cancellation of the policy. The audit may be performed through a physical examination of records at the insured's premises, located at 914 Millrace Parkway, Worcester, MA 01608, or via a remote documentation review. The insured must cooperate fully with the designated audit personnel.

If the final audited premium exceeds the estimated premium paid during the policy period, the named insured will be billed for the additional amount. Conversely, if the audited premium is less than the estimated premium, the carrier will issue a refund or apply the credit to subsequent policy periods. The experience modification factor of 1.04 and the schedule rating adjustment of 0% will be applied to the final audited manual premium.

References to classification, remuneration, and rating basis include NH class code 9015 only for the state and operation shown in the information page.

Headings are included for ease of reading and do not alter statutory benefits, employers liability limits, audit rights, or state amendatory provisions.

If a state endorsement and a general condition address the same subject, the state-specific endorsement controls for the affected state.

The insured should retain payroll journals, tax filings, subcontractor certificates, job-duty records, and officer status records used to support the classification entries.

Classification summaries on one page do not replace the information page, payroll schedule, endorsement schedule, or premium audit statement.

A certificate, binder note, invoice, or producer correspondence item does not amend a payroll or class-code entry unless an endorsement is issued.

Final premium may require allocation of remuneration by state, governing class, officer status, overtime treatment, and subcontracted work records.

When a class code appears on multiple schedules, the state, item identifier, and effective date should be used to read the entries together.

**SECTION A - RECORDS AND AUDIT**

The insured must keep payroll journals, tax filings, job-duty records, and contract labor records for Building operations by owner assigned to class code 9015 in NH.

The remuneration entry of $209,573 is an estimate for rating purposes and may be revised after audit without changing the coverage afforded by the policy.

Separate records are required when an employee performs duties that may fall under more than one classification or more than one covered state.

If adequate records are not available, remuneration may be assigned to the highest rated applicable classification permitted by the rating rules.

**SECTION B - STATE AND CLASSIFICATION CONDITIONS**

State amendatory endorsements, statutory benefit provisions, and assigned-risk rules apply before any conflicting general condition in this policy packet.

A classification shown on a schedule is not a warranty that all operations at the insured location are limited to that class.

Officer, partner, member, volunteer, leased-worker, and subcontractor treatment is determined by the attached endorsements and the applicable state rules.

Certificates from subcontractors must be available for audit and must identify the period of work, covered operations, and limits carried by the subcontractor.

ARGENT BIRCH EMPLOYERS PROVIDES THE COVERAGE DETAILED HEREIN TO THE NAMED INSURED, BLUE KETTLE FOOD SERVICE, LLC, WHOSE PRIMARY MAILING ADDRESS IS RECORDED AS 914 MILLRACE PARKWAY, WORCESTER, MA 01608. THE ADMINISTRATIVE PARAMETERS OF THIS CONTRACT ARE GOVERNED BY THE DECLARATIONS AND THE CORRESPONDING STATE-SPECIFIC SCHEDULES ATTACHED AT ISSUANCE. THE POLICY PERIOD COMMENCES ON 04/01/2026 AND CONCLUDES ON 04/01/2027, WITH ALL EFFECTIVE DATES BEGINNING AT STANDARD TIME AT THE PRIMARY MAILING ADDRESS OF THE NAMED INSURED.

This document establishes the foundational parameters for workers compensation and employers liability coverage across multiple jurisdictions. Operations are currently scheduled for the states of Connecticut and Massachusetts. The classification schedule assigns estimated remuneration to the states and class codes shown. Final premium may change if payroll records, job duties, or state assignments differ from the estimates used at issuance.

The experience modification factor of 1.04 and the schedule rating adjustment of 0% apply to the policy as a whole unless a state-specific endorsement provides otherwise. These rating elements are applied to the manual premium generated by the audited payroll to determine the final financial obligation of the named insured. Brindle Coast Coverage Group, operating under producer code PX-73916, serves as the designated representative for this transaction.

The employer must maintain detailed ledgers segregating remuneration by state and classification code. Argent Birch Employers retains the authority to examine and audit all financial records, tax documents, and employment contracts associated with Blue Kettle Food Service, LLC during the policy period and within three years following its expiration.

References to classification, remuneration, and rating basis include VT class code 5066 only for the state and operation shown in the information page.

Headings are included for ease of reading and do not alter statutory benefits, employers liability limits, audit rights, or state amendatory provisions.

If a state endorsement and a general condition address the same subject, the state-specific endorsement controls for the affected state.

The insured should retain payroll journals, tax filings, subcontractor certificates, job-duty records, and officer status records used to support the classification entries.

Classification summaries on one page do not replace the information page, payroll schedule, endorsement schedule, or premium audit statement.

A certificate, binder note, invoice, or producer correspondence item does not amend a payroll or class-code entry unless an endorsement is issued.

Final premium may require allocation of remuneration by state, governing class, officer status, overtime treatment, and subcontracted work records.

When a class code appears on multiple schedules, the state, item identifier, and effective date should be used to read the entries together.

SECTION A - RECORDS AND AUDIT

The insured must keep payroll journals, tax filings, job-duty records, and contract labor records for Contractor executive supervisor assigned to class code 5066 in VT.

Separate records are required when an employee performs duties that may fall under more than one classification or more than one covered state.

If adequate records are not available, remuneration may be assigned to the highest rated applicable classification permitted by the rating rules.

YW700400

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
ELECTRICAL OPERATIONS SAFETY ENDORSEMENT

Endorsement No. WC-EN-001                                                          Effective 01/01/2026

ITEM,WC-0001,STATE / CLASS,CT / 8810
CLASSIFICATION,Clerical office employees,PAYROLL / RATE,$45,136 / 0.42
PREMIUM,$189,FORM,WC 00 00 01 A 07 23
ENDORSEMENT,WC-EN-001,EFFECTIVE DATE,01/01/2026
MATERIALITY,Administrative,,

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

EFFECTIVE 04/01/2026, THIS ENDORSEMENT APPLIES SPECIFICALLY TO OPERATIONS CLASSIFIED UNDER CODE 5190 FOR ELECTRICAL WIRING WITHIN BUILDINGS. DUE TO THE INHERENT HAZARDS ASSOCIATED WITH THESE ACTIVITIES, ARGENT BIRCH EMPLOYERS REQUIRES THE IMPLEMENTATION OF SPECIFIC SAFETY PROTOCOLS TO MITIGATE THE RISK OF OCCUPATIONAL INJURIES. THIS ENDORSEMENT MODIFIES THE GENERAL POLICY CONDITIONS REGARDING EMPLOYER DUTIES.

Blue Kettle Food Service, LLC must ensure that all personnel engaged in electrical wiring activities maintain the appropriate state licensure and certifications required by the Commonwealth of Massachusetts. The named insured must verify the credentials of all employees and independent contractors prior to their commencement of electrical work at any job site.

The employer must provide and mandate the use of personal protective equipment, including arc flash suits, insulated gloves, and safety eyewear, for all individuals performing tasks under class code 5190. Furthermore, the named insured must implement a comprehensive lockout/tagout program to prevent the accidental energization of electrical circuits during maintenance or installation procedures.

Failure to adhere to the safety protocols outlined in this endorsement may result in the application of a safety penalty surcharge during the final premium audit. Argent Birch Employers retains the right to conduct unannounced safety inspections at any active job site to verify compliance with these requirements.

References to classification, remuneration, and rating basis include CT class code 8810 only for the state and operation shown in the information page.

Headings are included for ease of reading and do not alter statutory benefits, employers liability limits, audit rights, or state amendatory provisions.

If a state endorsement and a general condition address the same subject, the state-specific endorsement controls for the affected state.

The insured should retain payroll journals, tax filings, subcontractor certificates, job-duty records, and officer status records used to support the classification entries.

Classification summaries on one page do not replace the information page, payroll schedule, endorsement schedule, or premium audit statement.

A certificate, binder note, invoice, or producer correspondence item does not amend a payroll or class-code entry unless an endorsement is issued.

Final premium may require allocation of remuneration by state, governing class, officer status, overtime treatment, and subcontracted work records.

When a class code appears on multiple schedules, the state, item identifier, and effective date should be used to read the entries together.

SECTION A - RECORDS AND AUDIT

The insured must keep payroll journals, tax filings, job-duty records, and contract labor records for Clerical office employees assigned to class code 8810 in CT.

The remuneration entry of $45,136 is an estimate for rating purposes and may be revised after audit without changing the coverage afforded by the policy.

Separate records are required when an employee performs duties that may fall under more than one classification or more than one covered state.

If adequate records are not available, remuneration may be assigned to the highest rated applicable classification permitted by the rating rules.

SECTION B - STATE AND CLASSIFICATION CONDITIONS

State amendatory endorsements, statutory benefit provisions, and assigned-risk rules apply before any conflicting general condition in this policy packet.

A classification shown on a schedule is not a warranty that all operations at the insured location are limited to that class.

Officer, partner, member, volunteer, leased-worker, and subcontractor treatment is determined by the attached endorsements and the applicable state rules.

Certificates from subcontractors must be available for audit and must identify the period of work, covered operations, and limits carried by the subcontractor.
